   Rule Id: [34mBD000701[0m

  Severity: [36mImportant[0m, Confidence: [36mHigh[0m
  Filename: [33m/scrypt-0.8.27/README.rst[0m
   Pattern: [32m(npm owner|password|htpasswd|auth_?token|secret_?key|private_?key|authorized_keys?|npmrc|\.ssh|usersecrets?|api_?keys|nuget\.config|\.identityservice)[0m
[30;1m20 | [0m[35ma *minimum* amount of time to use when encrypting and decrypting. If,[0m
[30;1m21 | [0m[35mfor example, a password takes 0.05 seconds to verify, a user won't[0m
[30;1m22 | [0m[35mnotice the slight delay when signing in, but doing a brute force[0m
[30;1m23 | [0m[35msearch of several billion passwords will take a considerable amount of[0m
[30;1m24 | [0m[35mtime. This is in contrast to more traditional hash functions such as[0m
